RobotNum_total =

    10

var_runtime=zeros(RobotNum_total,1);

for i = 1 :RobotNum_total
    
    moyen(i)=mean(run_time_global{i,1});
    var_runtime(i)= std(run_time_global{i,1});
end

figure(2)

rob=1:1:RobotNum_total;

errorbar(rob,moyen,var_runtime,'-o');
